Aug 2020 10:30:50 +0000","feedId":1311,"bgimg":"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2021MarketingBudgetsImage600w.jpg","linkMd5":"4dadf9a9c6fa44d6bdedd7d004dd11a4","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn35@2020_6/2020/08/24/14-15-22-238_1a815011a9d7efa7.webp","destWidth":600,"destHeight":360,"sourceBytes":66147,"destBytes":24810,"author":"Alexis Hall","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/2021MarketingBudgetsImage600w.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn35@2020_6/2020/08/24/14-15-22-238_1a815011a9d7efa7.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/OnlineMarketingSEOBlog?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn11@2020_5/2020/08/24/14-15-22-140_b75958f276086430.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/OnlineMarketingSEOBlog/~4/spqLdPuGUAI":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn64@2020_5/2020/08/24/14-15-26-688_1f028543e841960d.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598278521855},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 22:15:21","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 22:15:21","title":"6 New Rules for B2B Marketing in the COVID-19 Era","link":"https://www.toprankblog.com/?p=28845","description":"<p><img width=\"600\" height=\"338\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/b2b-marketing-rules-covid19.jpg\" class=\"attachment-post-thumbnail size-post-thumbnail wp-post-image\" alt=\"B2B Marketing Rules Covid-19\" srcset=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/b2b-marketing-rules-covid19.jpg 600w, https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/b2b-marketing-rules-covid19-300x169.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 600px) 100vw, 600px\" /></p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28847\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/b2b-marketing-rules-covid19.jpg\" alt=\"B2B Marketing Rules Covid-19\" width=\"600\" height=\"338\" />\nI was supposed to go to an Alanis Morissette concert this July. When the pandemic hit hard in March, I wasn’t ready to cancel my ticket yet. Surely, </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">surely</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> we would have it sorted in time for an outdoor concert four months from now. I held out hope. Then, in June, she rescheduled for July, 2021. And now I’m wondering if </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">that</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> will be enough time.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Isn’t it ironic? </span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Don’t you think?</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">All of which to say: This pandemic has been around for longer than we thought it would, and is looking to linger far longer than we would like. What seemed like a brief, surreal interlude to be gotten through has now become a reality to live with, at least for the time being.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As B2B marketers, we need to reassess how we are adapting our marketing to our buyers’ current situation. We’re no longer scrambling to cobble together short-term fixes — we need to be out of reaction mode and into strategic planning mode.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our marketing agency has been helping clients <a href=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/2020/03/covid19-stop-b2b-marketing/\">revise their marketing plans</a> for months now, from messaging and audience to tactics and measurement. Here are a few rules we’ve picked up that other marketers should follow:</span>\n<h2><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">6 New Rules for B2B Marketing in the COVID-19 Era</span></h2>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #1: Always Be Relevant</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Okay, this is less a NEW rule than a timely reminder. I’m sure most marketers who read our blog (as smart, skilled and beautiful as you are) don’t need to hear it. But just in case: You should never come to an audience without something of value.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Corollary: “Something of value” can not equal “Knowledge of how our product/solution can improve your life.”</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">People are distracted and stressed. They’re dealing with a new crisis every day. They’re spending </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">way </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">more time with their children than is psychologically healthy. And they have more content than ever before to occupy their free time. If you’re asking for their attention, you must reward it. Be entertaining, be useful, be both if you can. [bctt tweet=\"'Be entertaining, be useful, be both if you can' in your #B2B content marketing, says @nitewrites.\" username=\"toprank\"]</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">After you deliver, then you can ask for a next step. But make sure your content is intrinsically valuable.</span>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #2: Encourage Interaction</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The pandemic lifestyle is, to put it lightly, isolating. Who would have thought you could miss hearing co-workers rock in their chairs, play music a little too loud, or bump into you in the hallway? Most of us are craving social interaction.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re used to broadcasting with your content, it’s time to consider how you can start conversations. How can you interact with your audience on a human level? How can you encourage them to interact with each other, too? Think how much your audience would value a lively, thought-provoking conversation with their colleagues and peers.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can encourage interaction with content in a few easy ways:</span>\n<ul>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Host a LinkedIn Live chat</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Run a Twitter chat</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Sponsor a topic-themed chat in a video conferencing app</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Run an </span><a href=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/2020/07/b2b-webinars-2020/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">interactive webinar</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In general, look for ways you can call out a subset of your audience and get them talking, both to each other and to your brand representatives. We can all use a little more social interaction right now.</span>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #3: Keep Messaging Empathetic</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">I don’t know about you, but I cringe every time I see an ad about something “going viral.” We are 6 months into a viral pandemic and marketers are still running ads about going viral! How can this be? </span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">This is just one example of how completely innocuous messaging pre-COVID can seem tone-deaf now. Does your content have an anecdote about a dinner party with 15 people? Does your header image feature a crowd of people? Are you talking about “going into the office” or “thinking about this on your commute?” If so, you’re alienating your audience.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Not every piece of content has to be about the pandemic, or being nostalgic for the world that once was. But there needs to be a </span><a href=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/2020/07/boosting-and-deepening-engagement-through-empathy-in-b2b-marketing/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">baseline of empathy</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">: Working from home, social distancing, and mask-wearing are all facts of everyday life.</span>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #4: Experiment with Formats</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">In the time before the pandemic, we all spent hours looking at screens every day. It’s just there were </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">different</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> screens, in different environments. It was easier to differentiate between the office and home, work and play. Now, our surroundings are homogenous throughout the day — and the content we consume feels same-y, too.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Think about content fatigue as you plan your calendar. Is your audience looking for another wall of text? Do they want to look at another grid of talking heads? </span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Our agency is finding more success right now with multimedia, interactive content. Our </span><a href=\"https://www.toprankmarketing.com/get-the-2020-b2b-influencer-marketing-report/?utm_source=Social&#38;utm_medium=Lee%20Odden&#38;utm_campaign=2025%20State%20of%20Influencer%20Marketing%20Report\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">B2B Influencer Marketing report</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> is an example. The content includes case studies, influencer participation, and original research, presented in an animated, dynamic way.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Essentially, keep in mind that idea of efficiently delivering value. Can your blog post be a quick video or audio interview instead? And can that video be five minutes long instead of 10?  [bctt tweet=\"Can your blog post be a quick video or audio interview instead? And can that video be five minutes long instead of 10? says @nitewrites.\" username=\"toprank\"]</span>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #5: Collaborate on Content</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">For me, one of the stranger elements of pandemic life is learning how similar I am to everyone else. I had an urge to do puzzles in March — all the stores were sold out. I wanted to make bread in April — the stores ran out of flour. In May, everyone bought bikes. </span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Right now, every B2B business is missing their trade shows and in-person demos. So most of them are doubling down on content. The best way to differentiate </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">your</span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\"> content is to bring your audience voices they can’t hear anywhere else.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Co-create content with influencers. Feature subject matter experts in your organization. Tap your current and prospective customers to get their take. The more voices you can bring to your content, the more it will stand out to your audience.</span>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Rule #6: Re-Align Measurement with Current Goals</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Per rule #1, people are less interested in promotional content right now. Businesses may have put their purchasing plans on hold, or at least tightened budgets. Marketing’s chief goal right now is likely to be establishing brand credibility, creating thought leadership content, and building relationships for the future.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">As your goals change, your measurement must change as well. You can’t measure an awareness campaign in SQLs, or relationship-building in number of demo requests received. That doesn’t mean giving up on measurement or accountability — it just means making the metrics match your goals. For example, you could measure:</span>\n<ul>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Brand share of voice</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Email/Blog subscribers</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Social media audience/interactions</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Content consumption metrics (time on page, scroll depth, links clicked)</span></li>\n \t<li style=\"font-weight: 400;\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Content resonance (backlinks and social shares)</span></li>\n</ul>\n<h3><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">How New Are These Rules?</span></h3>\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">So here’s the $100,000 (adjusted for inflation) question: At what point should you </span><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">stop </span></i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">producing relevant, interactive, empathetic, dynamic and collaborative content? When can you heave a sigh of relief, stop listening to your audience, and start broadcasting promotional messages?</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">When you put it that way, it’s obvious: These rules are best practices for content no matter what’s going on in the world. The pandemic didn’t create the need for these rules; it just amplified how crucial they are. Back in January, we might have had the luxury of ignoring one or more of them. Now we have the joyous necessity of being forced to do better.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">And that’s the good news: Making your marketing better for the pandemic will make you a better marketer now and for whatever comes next.</span>\n\n<span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Need help creating content? </span><a href=\"https://www.toprankmarketing.com/services/content-marketing/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">We’re here for you</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span><p>The post <a width=\"600\" height=\"360\" />\n\nAre you using the latest search engine optimization (SEO) tools to help with your content marketing efforts?\n\nDon't worry, as we’ve got you covered with a look at some of the most helpful SEO tools to help you refine and augment your content marketing plans.\n\nSorting through lists of the seemingly endless number of available SEO tools can be frustrating as well as a hit and miss proposition, however we’ve put this collection together so that you can skip the search and get right into SEO tools you can use today to help you create <a href=\"https://www.toprankmarketing.com/services/content-marketing/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">amazing content marketing stories</a>.\n\nLet’s jump in with our collection of fresh SEO tools to boost your content marketing experiences.\n<h2>1 — Google Lighthouse</h2>\n<img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28798\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/GoogleLighthouse600w.png\" alt=\"Google Lighthouse\" width=\"600\" height=\"290\" />\n\nGoogle’s own <a href=\"https://developers.google.com/web/tools/lighthouse\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Lighthouse</a> tool — an open-source project — offers a simple way to check a number of basic SEO-related issues that every website should consider. Among its auditing functions are tools specifically focusing on performance, SEO, accessibility, and progressive web apps, and it's also capable of examining webpages requiring authentication.\n\nThe tool can be run standalone, from the web, in Google's Chrome DevTools, or incorporated into continuous integration systems, and its Lighthouse Viewer allows viewing and sharing of analysis data online.\n<h2>2 — Botify SEO Platform</h2>\n<img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28799\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/Botify600w.png\" alt=\"Botify\" width=\"600\" height=\"327\" />\n\nThere are numerous powerful SEO platforms that each look to be as close to a one-stop-shop as possible for marketers and brands to gain reliable and relevant search insight, and squarely in this category is enterprise SEO suite company <a href=\"https://www.botify.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Botify</a>.\n\nBotify offers a vast array of SEO analysis, data crawling intelligence and indexing metrics tools, all while working to make this complex information both easy to understand and act on, as Google’s <a href=\"https://twitter.com/g33konaut\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Martin Splitt</a> recently <a href=\"https://www.botify.com/blog/martin-splitt-javascript-rendering\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">touched on</a> in a live video conversation.\n<h2>3 — Bing URL Submissions Plugin for WordPress</h2>\n<img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28800\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/Bing600w.png\" alt=\"Bing\" width=\"600\" height=\"366\" />\n\nB2B marketers in WordPress environments recently got access to an open-source plug-in from Bing Webmaster Tools, automating the submission of new site content to the Microsoft’s Bing search engine.\n\n<a href=\"https://blogs.bing.com/webmaster/july-2020/Get-your-WordPress-content-indexed-immediately-using-Bing-Webmaster-Tools-plugin/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Bing URL Submissions Plugin</a> in a feature-rich plug-in that can also be customized via Bing’s API for incorporation into other content management systems.\n<h2>4 — Schema.org</h2>\n<img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28801\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/Schema600w.png\" alt=\"Schema\" width=\"600\" height=\"366\" />\n\nGoogle and other search engine firms prefer that businesses use schema markup for structured data in the format set forth and maintained by the <a href=\"https://schema.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Schema.org</a> organization, which is especially important today as features including Google’s Knowledge Graphs rely in part on this simple yet often-overlooked element, as <a href=\"https://twitter.com/michalpecanek\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Michal Pecánek</a> recently <a href=\"https://ahrefs.com/blog/google-knowledge-graph/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">examined</a> for Ahrefs.\n<h2>5 — WebPagetest</h2>\n<img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-28802\" src=\"https://www.toprankblog.com/wp-content/uploads/WebPagetest600w.png\" alt=\"WebPagetest\" width=\"600\" height=\"305\" />\n\nAnother free tool frequently used by savvy search industry professionals is <a href=\"https://webpagetest.org/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">WebPagetest</a>, allowing webmasters and technically-proficient marketers to run a variety of tests including content type breakdowns, page speed data and others providing helpful information.\n\nThe data from WebPagetest can be used to troubleshoot website slowness issues, as <a href=\"https://twitter.com/rustybrick\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Barry Schwartz</a> recently outlined in “<a href=\"https://www.seroundtable.com/iagnose-largest-contentful-paint-lcp-slowness-29651.html\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Google: How To Diagnose Largest Contentful Paint (LCP) Slowness</a>.”\n<h2>Smart SEO Tools To Make You A Knowledge Builder</h2>\n<iframe class=\"giphy-embed\" src=\"https://giphy.com/embed/NN28qvpRYPVsc\" width=\"480\" height=\"360\" frameborder=\"0\" GIPHY</a>\n\nWe hope you’ve found at least a few new-to-you SEO content marketing tools among those we’ve taken a look at here, and that you’ll find them useful as you create new campaigns that are using the soundest practices of SEO, and that they'll also help build your own team’s knowledge.\n\nWe have a multi-year history of highlighting helpful marketing tools, and here are a few of the
